***назойливый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:назойливый.html>назо́йливый</a> (9714)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, original meaning may have been "noisy", in which case it may be derived from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">зой</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zoj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">scream</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ливый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-livyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">зои́ться</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zoítʹsja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rage, to rave</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Both <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">зой</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zoj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">зои́ться</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zoítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are ultimately related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зиять.html>зия́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zijátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to yawn, to gape</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назойливый.html>назо́йливый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nazójlivyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>irritating, intrusive, pushy</li></ol>

***назревать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:назревать.html>назрева́ть</a> (17208)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назреть.html>назре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nazrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назревать.html>назрева́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nazrevátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назреть.html>назре́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to ripen, to become ripe, to mature, (abscess) to come to a head</li>
<li>to be about to happen, to boil up, to be brewing</li></ol>

***назреть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:назреть.html>назре́ть</a> (24990)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зреть.html>зре́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zrétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назреть.html>назре́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nazrétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назревать.html>назрева́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to ripen, to become ripe, to mature, (abscess) to come to a head</li>
<li>to be about to happen, to boil up, to be brewing
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:назреть.html>назре́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">voprós <b>nazrél</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the question is ripe; the question cannot be put off</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кризис.html>кри́зис</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:назреть.html>назре́л</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krízis <b>nazrél</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">things have reached a crisis point; crisis is brewing</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:называться.html>называ́ться</a> (844)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:называть.html>называ́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nazyvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:называться.html>называ́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nazyvátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:назваться.html>назва́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to identify oneself, to give one’s name</li>
<li>to be called, to be named</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:называть.html>называ́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nazyvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***наивысший.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наивысший.html>наивы́сший</a> (16080)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">наи-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nai-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высший.html>вы́сший</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výsšij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наивысший.html>наивы́сший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naivýsšij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">superlative degree of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высокий.html>высо́кий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vysókij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: highest, greatest</li></ol>

***наигрывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наигрывать.html>наи́грывать</a> (25738)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">наигра́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naigrátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наигрывать.html>наи́грывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naígryvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">наигра́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to play (several songs, pieces or theatrical roles)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to gain (some money) gambling or playing a musical instrument</li>
<li>to play <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">quietly or only the main melody, on a musical instrument</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to play (a song or piece) for a recording</li>
<li>to record the music of (a record or film)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наизнанку.html>наизна́нку</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:выворачивать.html>вывора́чивает</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́того</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чувство.html>чу́встве</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:отвращение.html>отвраще́ния</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">menjá <b>naiznánku</b> vyvoráčivajet ot étovo (o čúvstve otvraščénija)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it turns my stomach</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***наитие.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наитие.html>наи́тие</a> (25683)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu"><a href = vnd.unilang:наитие.html>наи́тие</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">naitie</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; constructed as if <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>найти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">najtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-тие</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-tije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наитие.html>наи́тие</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">naítije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наитие.html>наи́тия</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наитие.html>наи́тия</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наитие.html>наи́тий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated or literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> heaven-sent inspiration</li></ol>

***найти.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>найти́</a> (211)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*najьti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">find</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Synchronically derivable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-йти́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>найти́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">najtí</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:находить.html>находи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to find
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2005</b>,  “<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>Вся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любовь.html>любо́вь</a></i></span>”, performed by t.A.T.u:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>найдёшь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нелюбимый.html>нелюби́мых</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дома́х</a><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нарваться.html>нарвёшься</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:страх.html>страх</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мина.html>ми́нах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:впотьмах.html>впотьма́х</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">i sebjá ne <b>najdjóšʹ</b> v neljubímyx domáx<br />i narvjóšʹsja na strax kak na mínax vpotʹmáx</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">And you will not find yourself in a unloved home<br />And you will run into fear like into mines in the dark</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to think, to consider</li>
<li>to come across</li>
<li>to be located, to be situated</li>
<li>to happen to have</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>найти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">najtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:найтись.html>найти́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">najtísʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:находиться.html>находи́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>найти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">najtí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span>: to happen to have, to be discovered
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">наконе́ц-то <b><a href = vnd.unilang:найтись.html>нашла́сь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мой.html>моя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́га</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>она́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>была́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:под.html>под</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кровать.html>крова́тью</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nakonéc-to <b>našlásʹ</b> mojá kníga. Oná bylá u menjá pod krovátʹju.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Finally, my book <b>is found</b>. It was under my bed.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наказание.html>наказа́ние</a> (2944)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказать.html>наказа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nakazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказание.html>наказа́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakazánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказание.html>наказа́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказание.html>наказа́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказание.html>наказа́ний</a></b>)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наказать.html>наказа́ть</a> (3949)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казать.html>каза́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказать.html>наказа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakazátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказывать.html>нака́зывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to punish</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bid, to order</li></ol>

***наказуемый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наказуемый.html>наказу́емый</a> (26934)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказать.html>наказа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nakazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-у́емый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-újemyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказуемый.html>наказу́емый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakazújemyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)наказу́емее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)наказу́емей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> punishable

***наказывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наказывать.html>нака́зывать</a> (7230)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказать.html>наказа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nakazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказывать.html>нака́зывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nakázyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наказать.html>наказа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to punish</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to bid, to order</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
